# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Summary

I've identified **18 key files** implementing exponential backoff retry patterns across the three repositories:

### **Kubernetes (kubernetes/kubernetes)** - 9 files
- **Core implementation**: `staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/wait/backoff.go` with `Backoff` struct and `ExponentialBackoff`/`ExponentialBackoffWithContext` functions
- **Specialized backoff**: `pkg/util/goroutinemap/exponentialbackoff/exponential_backoff.go` with exponential duration tracking (500ms → 2min 2sec max)
- **Webhook retries**: `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/webhook.go` with `WithExponentialBackoff` method
- **Volume operations**: Multiple reconcilers using the exponentialbackoff package for volume attachment/management

### **Grafana (grafana/grafana)** - 6 files
- **Git operations**: `apps/provisioning/pkg/repository/git/repository.go` using external `nanogit/retry.ExponentialBackoffRetrier` (8 attempts, 100ms-5s, 2.0x multiplier)
- **Alert evaluation**: `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/retry.go` with custom `exponentialBackoffRetryer` implementation
- **Generic retry**: `pkg/util/retryer/retryer.go` providing configurable exponential backoff helper

### **Prometheus (prometheus/prometheus)** - 3 files
- **Remote write queue**: `storage/remote/queue_manager.go` with `sendWriteRequestWithBackoff` function
- **Configuration**: `config/config.go` with `QueueConfig` defining MinBackoff (30ms) and MaxBackoff (5s)
- **Error classification**: `storage/remote/client.go` with `RecoverableError` type to distinguish transient from permanent failures

\"Exponential backoff retry implementations across three major Go projects demonstrate consistent patterns for handling transient failures.\\n\\nIn Kubernetes (kubernetes/kubernetes), exponential backoff is implemented in multiple layers: The core infrastructure in staging/src/k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/wait/backoff.go provides the Backoff struct and ExponentialBackoff/ExponentialBackoffWithContext functions that implement the exponential backoff algorithm using a delay function with configurable Duration, Factor, Jitter, Steps, and Cap. The pkg/util/goroutinemap/exponentialbackoff/exponential_backoff.go module provides a specialized ExponentialBackoff type for goroutine operations that tracks lastError, lastErrorTime, and durationBeforeRetry, doubling the wait duration on each failure until reaching maxDurationBeforeRetry (2 minutes 2 seconds). This pattern is used throughout the kubelet (volumemanager/reconciler, pluginmanager/reconciler) and volume attachment/detachment reconcilers. The staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/webhook.go implements WithExponentialBackoff for webhook retry logic.\\n\\nIn Grafana (grafana/grafana), exponential backoff appears in three distinct implementations: The apps/provisioning/pkg/repository/git/repository.go uses retry.ExponentialBackoffRetrier (imported from the external nanogit library) via the defaultGitRetrier function, configured with 8 total attempts (1 initial + 7 retries), 100ms initial delay, 5 second max delay, 2.0 multiplier, and jitter. The pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/retry.go implements a custom exponentialBackoffRetryer struct wrapping the backoff.BackOff interface, used for alert rule and recording rule evaluation with configurable max retries, initial/max delays, and clock support. The pkg/util/retryer/retryer.go provides a generic Retry function that uses exponential backoff starting from minDelay and increasing to maxDelay after each failure.\\n\\nIn Prometheus (prometheus/prometheus), exponential backoff is central to remote write resilience: The storage/remote/queue_manager.go implements sendWriteRequestWithBackoff that manages retry logic for write requests, starting with the minimum configured backoff and respecting Retry-After headers from remote endpoints. The config/config.go defines QueueConfig with MinBackoff (default 30ms) and MaxBackoff (default 5 seconds) fields that control the exponential backoff behavior during write failures. The storage/remote/client.go defines RecoverableError type to distinguish transient errors (500s, 429 rate limits, connection failures) that should trigger exponential backoff retry from permanent errors (4xx except 429) that should fail immediately.\"\n}\n",
